NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

This is to inform that the partnership of M/s Vamsa Engineering Works is being reconstituted as below:
Outgoing Partner:

Incoming Partner:
1. Ms. Sujatha Prakash
The continuing and incoming partners assume the entire assets and liabilities of M/s Vamsa Engineering Works and
the outgoing partner is not responsible for the affairs of M/s Vamsa Engineering Works with effect from 12th January 2017.

Chennai,
